# Kimi Vocabulary Expansion 500 - Clean Request

Generated: 2026-05-27T02:02:45.234Z

## Goal

Create exactly 500 K-2 vocabulary media pairs. Each row needs one exact-word image and one exact-word MP3 audio file. These words were curated from the LiteracyPath media audit and exclude existing approved exact image/audio pairs.

## Global Image Rules

- 1024x1024 WebP.
- Clean K-2 educational illustration.
- White or very pale background.
- Natural colours.
- No text, labels, letters, captions, or watermarks.
- No object faces or babyish/cutesy object characters.
- No sparkle/rainbow/fantasy styling unless the target word explicitly requires it.
- No busy background.
- Exact target word only.
- One centered object or one clearly staged action.

## Global Audio Rules

- MP3.
- Clear American English.
- Neutral adult female voice preferred.
- Say the target word only.
- No spelling.
- No phrase or sentence.
- Do not say "the" before the word.
- No music or sound effects.
- Normalized volume.
- Short silence before and after.

## Folder Structure

```text
public/media/vocabulary/images/{word}.webp
public/media/vocabulary/audio/{word}.mp3
manifest.json
```

Final Sounds /b/ words in Batch 1 should use the same vocabulary filenames here first. After QA approval, LiteracyPath can copy or reference them for skill-specific final-sounds paths as needed.

## Filename Rules

- Lowercase filenames.
- Use hyphens for multiword targets, e.g. `next-to.webp`.
- No spaces, uppercase letters, punctuation, version suffixes, or decorative descriptors.
- Image and audio stems must match exactly.

## Manifest Format

```json
{
  "word": "cub",
  "image": "/media/vocabulary/images/cub.webp",
  "audio": "/media/vocabulary/audio/cub.mp3",
  "batch": 1,
  "category": "final_sounds_b",
  "status": "generated"
}
```
